<user>115583519785164564980<//user>< Name>
Mary Arreola< /Name>
<Time>1544082111509< /Time><Rating>5< /Rating>< text>
It's a great place to hangout. The senior center provides lots of things to do.  Monday  is classic movie day. Weds  is bingo
Fridays is new movies.  Special luncheon for only $3. Free hair cuts. They have crafts, computer,  library  billards,  a gym, many other classes. A person can get the senior bus. Be left off and picked up. You could buy lunch or breakfast on certain days. You can also bring your own.  The center also sells coffee and snacks for less than 50 cents. They also offer excursions . You can read all about them in the Riverside parks & recreation magazine. The senior center is a great place to meet people and get social. The staff and volunteers are helpful and friendly.  Once a month the center gives out a bag or two of food items for free. The program is called food share
In the summer there is air conditioning.  In the winter there is heat. Come on down. Seniors in Riverside means 55 and up of age. No one has a time limit of how long you could hangout.  At least until closing.<//text>

2</Rating>
< Review>
Last week, I was quoted a specific price on a Tacoma over email by Mark Shehadi in sales. I called to confirm and was put in touch with Keyth, the sales manager, who confirmed that was the price. I put a deposit on the truck and drove 3 hours up to the dealership the next day to sign the papers.

When Scott Abel (Finance manager) and I sat down to do financing, I was informed that they couldn't sell the truck to me at the quoted price and said they could only sell it for MSRP.  We went back and forth for a bit and clearly weren't on the same page, so I got up and drove the 3 hours back home empty-handed.

I don't think I've ever felt so screwed over, for lack of a better phrase. I took off work, drove all the way up there, and had a friend take off work so he could drive my other pickup back home.

Maybe there was a lack of communication and it was an honest mistake or maybe they thought I wouldn't leave without a truck no matter the price after driving 3 hours, but it cost myself and my friend a whole day of our time, not to mention the lost hours at both of our jobs.

I did two stars instead of 1 because Scott ended up sending me a small check for my inconvenience.  It doesn't come close to covering my lost hours at work and doesn't give me my day back, but at least he tried to make it somewhat right.

I will say that Monica and Jesse in sales were a pleasure to talk to while I waited to do paperwork. Too bad we couldn't do business but I ended up purchasing a very similar truck (minor differences in options) at a dealer much closer to home for around the price I was initially quoted at CardinaleWay.<//Review>

I've probably visited Fork Over Pork over 15 times now. However, my review will be from a non-KBBQ experience, since myself and my friends have only eaten regular entrees here. (One day we will.)

Staff: Attentive and friendly
Food: Delicious! I typically get the kimchi rice or the bibimbap. My dining companion likes getting tofu soup, all varieties. Main complaint re:tofu soup is that there's not enough rice, and extra rice costs $2 per bowl.

<rating>5</rating><Review>I'm not korean but a real fan of their dishes :) We were craving for Biibimbap & gladly discovered this spot from Yelp with good reviews. < Review>
We just moved here to California and are early retirement full time RVers. I've been to quite a few Raleys in California but this one by far is the cleanest, well laid out, with lots of hidden gems and hard to find items I've ever seen. After complimenting it to the cashier, she told me they had remodeled a couple of years ago and all the employees were pretty proud of it. She thanked me for the compliment. I'm sure I probably wouldn't have shopped here when we were a six person family but not so much for slightly higher pricing (not all items and certainly not that much higher) but mostly because the kids would have distracted me from taking my time to look at everything. Just because a store is a chain doesn't mean they are all the same. Kudos, Raleys, Napa. Good job!!< /Review>
